Hibernate: 
    select
        a1_0.id,
        a1_0.address,
        a1_0.category,
        a1_0.created_at,
        a1_0.description,
        a1_0.destination_id,
        a1_0.duration_minutes,
        a1_0.estimated_cost,
        a1_0.estimated_duration,
        a1_0.is_custom,
        a1_0.latitude,
        a1_0.longitude,
        a1_0.name,
        a1_0.opening_hours,
        a1_0.phone,
        a1_0.photo_url,
        a1_0.place_id,
        a1_0.price_level,
        a1_0.rating,
        a1_0.reviews_json,
        a1_0.updated_at,
        a1_0.user_ratings_total,
        a1_0.website 
    from
        activities a1_0 
    where
        a1_0.destination_id=? 
    order by
        case 
            when a1_0.rating is not null 
            and a1_0.user_ratings_total>100 
                then ((a1_0.rating*log10(a1_0.user_ratings_total))*10) 
            when a1_0.rating is not null 
            and a1_0.user_ratings_total>10 
                then ((a1_0.rating*log10(a1_0.user_ratings_total))*5) 
            when a1_0.rating is not null 
                then (a1_0.rating*2) 
            else 0 
    end desc,
    a1_0.name 
fetch
    first ? rows only
